I recently had the opportunity to spend an unforgettable time at Kaiyuan Mingdu Resort, which left a deep impression on me and made me want to share my pleasant experience.

As soon as I entered the resort, I was attracted by its beautiful environment and exquisite layout. The architectural design of the resort is ingenious, combining traditional and modern styles, giving people a sense of both classical and fashionable beauty. The surrounding green landscape is even more refreshing, and every step is a beautiful picture.

The service level of Kaiyuan Mingdu Resort is also first-class. From the moment I checked in, I felt the enthusiasm and thoughtfulness of the staff. They not only patiently answered my questions, but also took the initiative to provide me with many useful travel suggestions. In the resort, I experienced meticulous care and thoughtful service, which made me feel the warmth of home.

The facilities of the resort are also complete, meeting all my needs during the vacation. The rooms are spacious and bright, and the decoration is elegant and comfortable, giving people a sense of tranquility and comfort. The swimming pool, gym, SPA and other facilities in the resort made me linger and enjoy the fun of vacation.

Of course, food is also an indispensable part of vacation. The restaurants in New Century Grand Resort offer a variety of delicious dishes, whether Chinese or Western, which are unforgettable. In particular, their special dishes are praised by people and add a lot of color to my vacation experience.

In general, New Century Grand Resort is a relaxing and relaxing resort. Whether it is the beautiful environment, first-class service, rich facilities or delicious food, I feel its unique charm. If you also want to find a good place to relax and enjoy the fun of vacation, then New Century Grand Resort is definitely a good choice. I strongly recommend everyone to come here to experience it!
